  parent_id: number;
}

type NodeType = 'all' | 'question' | 'answer' | 'comment';
type SortByValue = 'date_desc' | 'date_asc' | 'interactions_desc' | 'interactions_asc' | 'score_desc' | 'score_asc';

interface QueryParams {
  search?: string;
  nodeType?: NodeType;
  sortBy?: SortByValue;
}

// Helper function with proper typing
const buildQueryClauses = (
  search: string,
  nodeType: NodeType,
  sortBy: SortByValue
): { whereClause: string; orderByClause: string; params: any[] } => {
  const params: any[] = [];
  let whereClause = 'WHERE (p.state_string IS NULL OR p.state_string != "(deleted)")';
  
  // Node type filter with proper type checking
  if (nodeType && nodeType !== 'all') {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = ?';
    params.push(nodeType);
  } else {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = "question"';
  }

  // Search filter
  if (search) {
    whereClause += ` AND (
      p.title LIKE ? OR 
      p.body LIKE ? OR 
      p.tagnames LIKE ?
    )`;
    const searchTerm = `%${search}%`;
    params.push(searchTerm, searchTerm, searchTerm);
  }

  // Sort clause with proper type checking
  let orderByClause = '';
  switch (sortBy) {
    case 'date_asc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY p.added_at ASC';
      break;
    case 'interactions_desc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY (answer_count + comment_count) DESC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'interactions_asc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY (answer_count + comment_count) ASC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'score_desc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY p.score DESC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'score_asc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY p.score ASC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    default:
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY p.added_at DESC';
  }

  return { whereClause, orderByClause, params };
};

// Update the endpoint to use the new types
app.get("/api/posts", async (req: Request<{}, {}, {}, QueryParams>, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const page = parseInt(String(req.query.page)) || 1;
    const limit = parseInt(String(req.query.limit)) || 10;
    const search = String(req.query.search || '');
    const nodeType = (req.query.nodeType || 'all') as NodeType;
    const sortBy = (req.query.sortBy || 'date_desc') as SortByValue;
    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;

    // ... rest of the endpoint code remains the same

    const { whereClause, orderByClause, params } = buildQueryClauses(
      search,
      nodeType,
      sortBy
    );

    // Updated query with filters and sorting
    const [rows] = await pool.query<ForumPostRow[]>(
      `SELECT 
        p.id, 
        p.title, 
        p.tagnames, 
        p.body,
        p.node_type,
        p.added_at, 
        p.score,
        (
          SELECT COUNT(*) 
          FROM forum_posts_raw answers 
          WHERE answers.parent_id = p.id 
            AND answers.node_type = 'answer'
            AND (answers.state_string IS NULL OR answers.state_string != '(deleted)')
        ) as answer_count,
        (
          SELECT COUNT(*) 
          FROM forum_posts_raw comments 
          WHERE comments.parent_id = p.id 
            AND comments.node_type = 'comment'
            AND (comments.state_string IS NULL OR comments.state_string != '(deleted)')
        ) as comment_count
      FROM forum_posts_raw p
      ${whereClause}
      GROUP BY p.id, p.title, p.tagnames, p.body, p.node_type, p.added_at, p.score
      ${orderByClause}
      LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`,
      [...params, limit, offset]
    );

    // Get total count with filters
    const [countResult] = await pool.query<TotalCountRow[]>(
      `SELECT COUNT(*) as total 
       FROM forum_posts_raw p
       ${whereClause}`,
      params
    );

    const total = countResult[0].total;
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / limit);

    // Ensure counts are numbers
    const formattedRows = rows.map(row => ({
      ...row,
      answer_count: Number(row.answer_count),
      comment_count: Number(row.comment_count)
    }));

    const response: ApiResponse<ForumPost[]> = {
      data: formattedRows,
      total,
      page,
      totalPages,
      filters: {
        search,
        nodeType: nodeType || 'all',
        tags: []
      },
      sort: sortBy
    };

    res.json(response);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Detailed API Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ 
      error: "Internal server error", 
      details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
    });
  }
});

import { RowDataPacket } from 'mysql2';

export type NodeType = 'all' | 'question' | 'answer' | 'comment';
export type SortByValue = 'date_desc' | 'date_asc' | 'interactions_desc' | 'interactions_asc' | 'score_desc' | 'score_asc';

export interface ForumPost {
    id: number;
    title: string;
    tagnames: string;
    body: string;
    node_type: string;
    added_at: Date;
    score: number;
    parent_id?: number;
    state_string?: string;
    answer_count: number;
    comment_count: number;
}

export interface Comment {
    id: number;
    body: string;
    node_type: string;
    added_at: Date;
    score: number;
    parent_id: number;
}

export interface QueryParams {
    page?: number;
    limit?: number;
    search?: string;
    nodeType?: NodeType;
    sortBy?: SortByValue;
}

export interface ApiResponse<T> {
    data: T;
    total: number;
    page: number;
    totalPages: number;
    filters?: {
        search: string;
        nodeType: NodeType;
        tags: string[];
    };
    sort?: SortByValue;
}

export interface CommentsResponse {
    comments: Comment[];
    post: ForumPost;
}

// Database specific interfaces
export interface ForumPostRow extends ForumPost, RowDataPacket {}
export interface CommentRow extends Comment, RowDataPacket {}
export interface TotalCountRow extends RowDataPacket {
    total: number;
}

export const Posts: React.FC = () => {
  const [posts, setPosts] = useState<ForumPost[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [totalPages, setTotalPages] = useState(1);
  
  // New state for filters
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [nodeType, setNodeType] = useState<NodeType>('all');
  const [sortBy, setSortBy] = useState<SortByValue>('date_desc');
  const [debouncedSearch, setDebouncedSearch] = useState('');

  // Debounce search input
  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      setDebouncedSearch(search);
    }, 500);

    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [search]);

  const fetchPosts = async (pageNumber: number) => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const queryParams = new URLSearchParams({
        page: pageNumber.toString(),
        limit: '10',
        search: debouncedSearch,
        nodeType,
        sortBy,
      });

      const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/posts?${queryParams}`);
      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      }
      const data: ApiResponse<ForumPost[]> = await response.json();
      setPosts(data.data);
      setTotalPages(data.totalPages);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching posts:', error);
      setError(error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'An error occurred');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    setPage(1); // Reset page when filters change
    fetchPosts(1);
  }, [debouncedSearch, nodeType, sortBy]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchPosts(page);
  }, [page]);

  const handlePageChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<unknown>, value: number) => {
    setPage(value);
  };

  const handleSearchChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    setSearch(event.target.value);
  };

  const handleNodeTypeChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<{ value: unknown }>) => {
    setNodeType(event.target.value as NodeType);
  };

  const handleSortChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<{ value: unknown }>) => {
    setSortBy(event.target.value as SortByValue);
  };

  return (
    <Box sx={{ maxWidth: '100%', margin: '0 auto', padding: 2 }}>
      <Typography variant="h4" gutterBottom align="center">
        Ayn Rand Forum Posts
      </Typography>

      {/* Filters Section */}
      <Stack 
        direction={{ xs: 'column', sm: 'row' }} 
        spacing={2} 
        sx={{ mb: 3 }}
        alignItems="center"
      >
        <TextField
          label="Search"
          variant="outlined"
          value={search}
          onChange={handleSearchChange}
          size="small"
          sx={{ minWidth: 200 }}
          InputProps={{
            startAdornment: (
              <InputAdornment position="start">
                <SearchIcon />
              </InputAdornment>
            ),
          }}
        />

        <FormControl size="small" sx={{ minWidth: 120 }}>
          <InputLabel>Type</InputLabel>
          <Select
            value={nodeType}
            label="Type"
            onChange={handleNodeTypeChange}
          >
            {NODE_TYPES.map(type => (
              <MenuItem key={type.value} value={type.value}>
                {type.label}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>

        <FormControl size="small" sx={{ minWidth: 150 }}>
          <InputLabel>Sort By</InputLabel>
          <Select
            value={sortBy}
            label="Sort By"
            onChange={handleSortChange}
          >
            {SORT_OPTIONS.map(option => (
              <MenuItem key={option.value} value={option.value}>
                {option.label}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>
      </Stack>

      {loading ? (
        <Box display="flex" justifyContent="center" alignItems="center" minHeight="200px">
          <CircularProgress />
        </Box>
      ) : error ? (
        <Typography color="error" align="center">
          Error: {error}
        </Typography>
      ) : !posts.length ? (
        <Typography align="center">
          No posts found
        </Typography>
      ) : (
        <>
          <TableContainer component={Paper}>
            <Table>
              <TableHead>
                <TableRow>
                  <TableCell width={50} />
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Title</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Tags</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Date</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }} align="right">Score</TableCell>
                </TableRow>
              </TableHead>
              <TableBody>
                {posts.map((post) => (
                  <Row key={post.id} post={post} />
                ))}
              </TableBody>
            </Table>
          </TableContainer>
          <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', marginTop: 2 }}>
            <Pagination 
              count={totalPages} 
              page={page} 
              onChange={handlePageChange}
              color="primary"
            />
          </Box>
        </>
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

import React, { useEffect, useState, ChangeEvent } from 'react';
import { 
  Table, 
  TableBody, 
  TableCell, 
  TableContainer, 
  TableHead, 
  TableRow, 
  Paper,
  Typography,
  CircularProgress,
  Pagination,
  Box,
  Chip,
  IconButton,
  Collapse,
  Badge,
  TextField,
  Select,
  MenuItem,
  FormControl,
  InputLabel,
  Stack,
  InputAdornment,
  SelectChangeEvent,
} from '@mui/material';
import SearchIcon from '@mui/icons-material/Search';
import KeyboardArrowDownIcon from '@mui/icons-material/KeyboardArrowDown';
import KeyboardArrowUpIcon from '@mui/icons-material/KeyboardArrowUp';
import { ForumPost, Comment, ApiResponse, CommentsResponse } from '../types';

// Define these types in the component since they're UI-specific
type NodeType = 'all' | 'question' | 'answer' | 'comment';
type SortByValue = 'date_desc' | 'date_asc' | 'interactions_desc' | 'interactions_asc' | 'score_desc' | 'score_asc';

interface RowProps {
  post: ForumPost;
}

const Row: React.FC<RowProps> = ({ post }) => {
  // Row component code remains the same...
};

const SORT_OPTIONS = [
  { value: 'date_desc', label: 'Newest First' },
  { value: 'date_asc', label: 'Oldest First' },
  { value: 'interactions_desc', label: 'Most Interactions' },
  { value: 'interactions_asc', label: 'Least Interactions' },
  { value: 'score_desc', label: 'Highest Score' },
  { value: 'score_asc', label: 'Lowest Score' },
] as const;

const NODE_TYPES = [
  { value: 'all', label: 'All Types' },
  { value: 'question', label: 'Questions' },
  { value: 'answer', label: 'Answers' },
  { value: 'comment', label: 'Comments' },
] as const;

export const Posts: React.FC = () => {
  const [posts, setPosts] = useState<ForumPost[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [totalPages, setTotalPages] = useState(1);
  
  // New state for filters
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [nodeType, setNodeType] = useState<NodeType>('all');
  const [sortBy, setSortBy] = useState<SortByValue>('date_desc');
  const [debouncedSearch, setDebouncedSearch] = useState('');

  // Debounce search input
  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      setDebouncedSearch(search);
    }, 500);

    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [search]);

  const fetchPosts = async (pageNumber: number) => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const queryParams = new URLSearchParams({
        page: pageNumber.toString(),
        limit: '10',
        search: debouncedSearch,
        nodeType,
        sortBy,
      });

      const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/posts?${queryParams}`);
      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      }
      const data: ApiResponse<ForumPost[]> = await response.json();
      setPosts(data.data);
      setTotalPages(data.totalPages);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching posts:', error);
      setError(error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'An error occurred');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    setPage(1);
    fetchPosts(1);
  }, [debouncedSearch, nodeType, sortBy]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchPosts(page);
  }, [page]);

  const handlePageChange = (_event: React.ChangeEvent<unknown>, value: number) => {
    setPage(value);
  };

  const handleSearchChange = (event: ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    setSearch(event.target.value);
  };

  const handleNodeTypeChange = (event: SelectChangeEvent<NodeType>) => {
    setNodeType(event.target.value as NodeType);
  };

  const handleSortChange = (event: SelectChangeEvent<SortByValue>) => {
    setSortBy(event.target.value as SortByValue);
  };

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <Box display="flex" justifyContent="center" alignItems="center" minHeight="200px">
        <CircularProgress />
      </Box>
    );
  }

  if (error) {
    return (
      <Typography color="error" align="center">
        Error: {error}
      </Typography>
    );
  }

  return (
    <Box sx={{ maxWidth: '100%', margin: '0 auto', padding: 2 }}>
      <Typography variant="h4" gutterBottom align="center">
        Ayn Rand Forum Posts
      </Typography>

      <Stack 
        direction={{ xs: 'column', sm: 'row' }} 
        spacing={2} 
        sx={{ mb: 3 }}
        alignItems="center"
      >
        <TextField
          label="Search"
          variant="outlined"
          value={search}
          onChange={handleSearchChange}
          size="small"
          sx={{ minWidth: 200 }}
          InputProps={{
            startAdornment: (
              <InputAdornment position="start">
                <SearchIcon />
              </InputAdornment>
            ),
          }}
        />

        <FormControl size="small" sx={{ minWidth: 120 }}>
          <InputLabel>Type</InputLabel>
          <Select<NodeType>
            value={nodeType}
            label="Type"
            onChange={handleNodeTypeChange}
          >
            {NODE_TYPES.map(type => (
              <MenuItem key={type.value} value={type.value}>
                {type.label}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>

        <FormControl size="small" sx={{ minWidth: 150 }}>
          <InputLabel>Sort By</InputLabel>
          <Select<SortByValue>
            value={sortBy}
            label="Sort By"
            onChange={handleSortChange}
          >
            {SORT_OPTIONS.map(option => (
              <MenuItem key={option.value} value={option.value}>
                {option.label}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>
      </Stack>

      {!posts.length ? (
        <Typography align="center">
          No posts found
        </Typography>
      ) : (
        <>
          <TableContainer component={Paper}>
            <Table>
              <TableHead>
                <TableRow>
                  <TableCell width={50} />
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Title</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Tags</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Date</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }} align="right">Score</TableCell>
                </TableRow>
              </TableHead>
              <TableBody>
                {posts.map((post) => (
                  <Row key={post.id} post={post} />
                ))}
              </TableBody>
            </Table>
          </TableContainer>
          <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', marginTop: 2 }}>
            <Pagination 
              count={totalPages} 
              page={page} 
              onChange={handlePageChange}
              color="primary"
            />
          </Box>
        </>
      )}
    </Box>
  );

I see the error - it's about the Row component's type definition. Let's fix that by properly typing the FC (Function Component) with RowProps. Here's the corrected Row component definition:

typescript
CopyInsert
const Row = React.memo(({ post }: RowProps) => {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [comments, setComments] = useState<Comment[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const fetchComments = async () => {
    if (!open) {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/posts/${post.id}/comments`);
        if (!response.ok) {
          throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
        }
        const data: CommentsResponse = await response.json();
        setComments(data.comments);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching comments:', error);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
    setOpen(!open);
  };

  return (
    <>
      <TableRow sx={{ '& > *': { borderBottom: 'unset' } }} hover>
        <TableCell>
          <Badge 
            badgeContent={(post.answer_count || 0) + (post.comment_count || 0)} 
            color="primary"
            sx={{ '& .MuiBadge-badge': { right: -3, top: 13 } }}
          >
            <IconButton
              aria-label="expand row"
              size="small"
              onClick={fetchComments}
            >
              {open ? <KeyboardArrowUpIcon /> : <KeyboardArrowDownIcon />}
            </IconButton>
          </Badge>
        </TableCell>
        <TableCell sx={{ maxWidth: 300 }}>
          <Typography variant="body1">
            {post.title || 'Untitled'}
          </Typography>
          <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary">
            {post.answer_count || 0} answers • {post.comment_count || 0} comments
          </Typography>
        </TableCell>
        <TableCell>
          {post.tagnames ? post.tagnames.split(' ').map((tag, i) => (
            <Chip 
              key={i} 
              label={tag} 
              size="small" 
              sx={{ m: 0.5 }} 
              variant="outlined"
            />
          )) : '-'}
        </TableCell>
        <TableCell>
          {post.added_at ? 
            new Date(post.added_at).toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
              year: 'numeric',
              month: 'short',
              day: 'numeric'
            }) : 'No date'
          }
        </TableCell>
        <TableCell align="right">
          {post.score || 0}
        </TableCell>
      </TableRow>
      <TableRow>
        <TableCell style={{ paddingBottom: 0, paddingTop: 0 }} colSpan={6}>
          <Collapse in={open} timeout="auto" unmountOnExit>
            <Box sx={{ margin: 1 }}>
              <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom component="div">
                Discussion Thread
              </Typography>
              {loading ? (
                <Box display="flex" justifyContent="center" p={2}>
                  <CircularProgress size={24} />
                </Box>
              ) : comments.length > 0 ? (
                <Table size="small">
                  <TableHead>
                    <TableRow>
                      <TableCell>Content</TableCell>
                      <TableCell>Type</TableCell>
                      <TableCell>Date</TableCell>
                      <TableCell align="right">Score</TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                  </TableHead>
                  <TableBody>
                    {comments.map((comment) => (
                      <TableRow 
                        key={comment.id} 
                        hover
                        sx={{
                          backgroundColor: comment.node_type === 'answer' ? 'action.hover' : 'inherit'
                        }}
                      >
                        <TableCell sx={{ maxWidth: 400 }}>
                          <Typography variant="body2">
                            {comment.body}
                          </Typography>
                        </TableCell>
                        <TableCell>
                          <Chip 
                            label={comment.node_type}
                            size="small"
                            color={comment.node_type === 'answer' ? 'success' : 'default'}
                          />
                        </TableCell>
                        <TableCell>
                          {new Date(comment.added_at).toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
                            year: 'numeric',
                            month: 'short',
                            day: 'numeric'
                          })}
                        </TableCell>
                        <TableCell align="right">{comment.score}</TableCell>
                      </TableRow>
                    ))}
                  </TableBody>
                </Table>
              ) : (
                <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary" align="center">
                  No responses yet
                </Typography>
              )}
            </Box>
          </Collapse>
        </TableCell>
      </TableRow>
    </>
  );
});

import React, { useEffect, useState, ChangeEvent } from 'react';
import { 
  Table, 
  TableBody, 
  TableCell, 
  TableContainer, 
  TableHead, 
  TableRow, 
  Paper,
  Typography,
  CircularProgress,
  Pagination,
  Box,
  Chip,
  IconButton,
  Collapse,
  Badge,
  TextField,
  Select,
  MenuItem,
  FormControl,
  InputLabel,
  Stack,
  InputAdornment,
  SelectChangeEvent,
} from '@mui/material';
import SearchIcon from '@mui/icons-material/Search';
import KeyboardArrowDownIcon from '@mui/icons-material/KeyboardArrowDown';
import KeyboardArrowUpIcon from '@mui/icons-material/KeyboardArrowUp';
import { ForumPost, Comment, ApiResponse, CommentsResponse } from '../types';

// Define these types in the component since they're UI-specific
type NodeType = 'all' | 'question' | 'answer' | 'comment';
type SortByValue = 'date_desc' | 'date_asc' | 'interactions_desc' | 'interactions_asc' | 'score_desc' | 'score_asc';

interface RowProps {
  post: ForumPost;
}

const Row = React.memo(({ post }: RowProps) => {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [comments, setComments] = useState<Comment[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const fetchComments = async () => {
    if (!open) {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/posts/${post.id}/comments`);
        if (!response.ok) {
          throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
        }
        const data: CommentsResponse = await response.json();
        setComments(data.comments);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching comments:', error);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
    setOpen(!open);
  };

  return (
    <>
      <TableRow sx={{ '& > *': { borderBottom: 'unset' } }} hover>
        <TableCell>
          <Badge 
            badgeContent={(post.answer_count || 0) + (post.comment_count || 0)} 
            color="primary"
            sx={{ '& .MuiBadge-badge': { right: -3, top: 13 } }}
          >
            <IconButton
              aria-label="expand row"
              size="small"
              onClick={fetchComments}
            >
              {open ? <KeyboardArrowUpIcon /> : <KeyboardArrowDownIcon />}
            </IconButton>
          </Badge>
        </TableCell>
        <TableCell sx={{ maxWidth: 300 }}>
          <Typography variant="body1">
            {post.title || 'Untitled'}
          </Typography>
          <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary">
            {post.answer_count || 0} answers • {post.comment_count || 0} comments
          </Typography>
        </TableCell>
        <TableCell>
          {post.tagnames ? post.tagnames.split(' ').map((tag, i) => (
            <Chip 
              key={i} 
              label={tag} 
              size="small" 
              sx={{ m: 0.5 }} 
              variant="outlined"
            />
          )) : '-'}
        </TableCell>
        <TableCell>
          {post.added_at ? 
            new Date(post.added_at).toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
              year: 'numeric',
              month: 'short',
              day: 'numeric'
            }) : 'No date'
          }
        </TableCell>
        <TableCell align="right">
          {post.score || 0}
        </TableCell>
      </TableRow>
      <TableRow>
        <TableCell style={{ paddingBottom: 0, paddingTop: 0 }} colSpan={6}>
          <Collapse in={open} timeout="auto" unmountOnExit>
            <Box sx={{ margin: 1 }}>
              <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom component="div">
                Discussion Thread
              </Typography>
              {loading ? (
                <Box display="flex" justifyContent="center" p={2}>
                  <CircularProgress size={24} />
                </Box>
              ) : comments.length > 0 ? (
                <Table size="small">
                  <TableHead>
                    <TableRow>
                      <TableCell>Content</TableCell>
                      <TableCell>Type</TableCell>
                      <TableCell>Date</TableCell>
                      <TableCell align="right">Score</TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                  </TableHead>
                  <TableBody>
                    {comments.map((comment) => (
                      <TableRow 
                        key={comment.id} 
                        hover
                        sx={{
                          backgroundColor: comment.node_type === 'answer' ? 'action.hover' : 'inherit'
                        }}
                      >
                        <TableCell sx={{ maxWidth: 400 }}>
                          <Typography variant="body2">
                            {comment.body}
                          </Typography>
                        </TableCell>
                        <TableCell>
                          <Chip 
                            label={comment.node_type}
                            size="small"
                            color={comment.node_type === 'answer' ? 'success' : 'default'}
                          />
                        </TableCell>
                        <TableCell>
                          {new Date(comment.added_at).toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
                            year: 'numeric',
                            month: 'short',
                            day: 'numeric'
                          })}
                        </TableCell>
                        <TableCell align="right">{comment.score}</TableCell>
                      </TableRow>
                    ))}
                  </TableBody>
                </Table>
              ) : (
                <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary" align="center">
                  No responses yet
                </Typography>
              )}
            </Box>
          </Collapse>
        </TableCell>
      </TableRow>
    </>
  );
});

Row.displayName = 'Row';

const SORT_OPTIONS = [
  { value: 'date_desc', label: 'Newest First' },
  { value: 'date_asc', label: 'Oldest First' },
  { value: 'interactions_desc', label: 'Most Interactions' },
  { value: 'interactions_asc', label: 'Least Interactions' },
  { value: 'score_desc', label: 'Highest Score' },
  { value: 'score_asc', label: 'Lowest Score' },
] as const;

const NODE_TYPES = [
  { value: 'all', label: 'All Types' },
  { value: 'question', label: 'Questions' },
  { value: 'answer', label: 'Answers' },
  { value: 'comment', label: 'Comments' },
] as const;

export const Posts: React.FC = () => {
  const [posts, setPosts] = useState<ForumPost[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [totalPages, setTotalPages] = useState(1);
  
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [nodeType, setNodeType] = useState<NodeType>('all');
  const [sortBy, setSortBy] = useState<SortByValue>('date_desc');
  const [debouncedSearch, setDebouncedSearch] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      setDebouncedSearch(search);
    }, 500);

    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [search]);

  const fetchPosts = async (pageNumber: number) => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const queryParams = new URLSearchParams({
        page: pageNumber.toString(),
        limit: '10',
        search: debouncedSearch,
        nodeType,
        sortBy,
      });

      const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/posts?${queryParams}`);
      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      }
      const data: ApiResponse<ForumPost[]> = await response.json();
      setPosts(data.data);
      setTotalPages(data.totalPages);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching posts:', error);
      setError(error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'An error occurred');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    setPage(1);
    fetchPosts(1);
  }, [debouncedSearch, nodeType, sortBy]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchPosts(page);
  }, [page]);

  const handlePageChange = (_event: React.ChangeEvent<unknown>, value: number) => {
    setPage(value);
  };

  const handleSearchChange = (event: ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    setSearch(event.target.value);
  };

  const handleNodeTypeChange = (event: SelectChangeEvent<NodeType>) => {
    setNodeType(event.target.value as NodeType);
  };

  const handleSortChange = (event: SelectChangeEvent<SortByValue>) => {
    setSortBy(event.target.value as SortByValue);
  };

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <Box display="flex" justifyContent="center" alignItems="center" minHeight="200px">
        <CircularProgress />
      </Box>
    );
  }

  if (error) {
    return (
      <Typography color="error" align="center">
        Error: {error}
      </Typography>
    );
  }

  return (
    <Box sx={{ maxWidth: '100%', margin: '0 auto', padding: 2 }}>
      <Typography variant="h4" gutterBottom align="center">
        Ayn Rand Forum Posts
      </Typography>

      <Stack 
        direction={{ xs: 'column', sm: 'row' }} 
        spacing={2} 
        sx={{ mb: 3 }}
        alignItems="center"
      >
        <TextField
          label="Search"
          variant="outlined"
          value={search}
          onChange={handleSearchChange}
          size="small"
          sx={{ minWidth: 200 }}
          InputProps={{
            startAdornment: (
              <InputAdornment position="start">
                <SearchIcon />
              </InputAdornment>
            ),
          }}
        />

        <FormControl size="small" sx={{ minWidth: 120 }}>
          <InputLabel>Type</InputLabel>
          <Select<NodeType>
            value={nodeType}
            label="Type"
            onChange={handleNodeTypeChange}
          >
            {NODE_TYPES.map(type => (
              <MenuItem key={type.value} value={type.value}>
                {type.label}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>

        <FormControl size="small" sx={{ minWidth: 150 }}>
          <InputLabel>Sort By</InputLabel>
          <Select<SortByValue>
            value={sortBy}
            label="Sort By"
            onChange={handleSortChange}
          >
            {SORT_OPTIONS.map(option => (
              <MenuItem key={option.value} value={option.value}>
                {option.label}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>
      </Stack>

      {!posts.length ? (
        <Typography align="center">
          No posts found
        </Typography>
      ) : (
        <>
          <TableContainer component={Paper}>
            <Table>
              <TableHead>
                <TableRow>
                  <TableCell width={50} />
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Title</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Tags</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Date</TableCell>
                  <TableCell sx={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }} align="right">Score</TableCell>
                </TableRow>
              </TableHead>
              <TableBody>
                {posts.map((post) => (
                  <Row key={post.id} post={post} />
                ))}
              </TableBody>
            </Table>
          </TableContainer>
          <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', marginTop: 2 }}>
            <Pagination 
              count={totalPages} 
              page={page} 
              onChange={handlePageChange}
              color="primary"
            />
          </Box>
        </>
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

I see what you mean. Looking at your screenshot, searching for "Objectivism" should definitely return more relevant results. Let's improve the search functionality in the backend.

Let's enhance the search in server/src/index.ts to:

Use MySQL's FULLTEXT search for better relevance

Here's the improved version:

typescript
CopyInsert
// In the buildQueryClauses function:
const buildQueryClauses = (
  search: string,
  nodeType: NodeType,
  sortBy: SortByValue
): { whereClause: string; orderByClause: string; params: any[] } => {
  const params: any[] = [];
  let whereClause = 'WHERE (p.state_string IS NULL OR p.state_string != "(deleted)")';
  
  // Node type filter remains the same
  if (nodeType && nodeType !== 'all') {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = ?';
    params.push(nodeType);
  } else {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = "question"';
  }

  // Improved search functionality
  if (search) {
    const searchTerms = search.trim().split(/\s+/).filter(term => term.length > 0);
    if (searchTerms.length > 0) {
      const searchClauses: string[] = [];
      searchTerms.forEach(term => {
        const searchTerm = `%${term}%`;
        searchClauses.push(`(
          LOWER(p.title) LIKE LOWER(?) OR
          LOWER(p.body) LIKE LOWER(?) OR
          LOWER(p.tagnames) LIKE LOWER(?) OR
          EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM forum_posts_raw child
            WHERE child.parent_id = p.id
            AND LOWER(child.body) LIKE LOWER(?)
          )
        )`);
        params.push(searchTerm, searchTerm, searchTerm, searchTerm);
      });
      whereClause += ` AND (${searchClauses.join(' AND ')})`;
    }
  }

  // Enhanced sorting with relevance when searching
  let orderByClause = '';
  if (search && search.trim()) {
    // When searching, prioritize matches in title and tags
    orderByClause = `
      ORDER BY 
        CASE 
          WHEN LOWER(p.title) LIKE LOWER(?) THEN 3
          WHEN LOWER(p.tagnames) LIKE LOWER(?) THEN 2
          ELSE 1
        END DESC,
    `;
    params.push(`%${search}%`, `%${search}%`);
  }

  // Append the regular sort criteria
  switch (sortBy) {
    case 'date_asc':
      orderByClause += 'p.added_at ASC';
      break;
    case 'interactions_desc':
      orderByClause += '(answer_count + comment_count) DESC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'interactions_asc':
      orderByClause += '(answer_count + comment_count) ASC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'score_desc':
      orderByClause += 'p.score DESC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'score_asc':
      orderByClause += 'p.score ASC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    default:
      orderByClause += 'p.added_at DESC';
  }

  return { whereClause, orderByClause, params };
};

// Update the main query to include the search ranking
const [rows] = await pool.query<ForumPostRow[]>(
  `SELECT 
    p.id, 
    p.title, 
    p.tagnames, 
    p.body,
    p.node_type,
    p.added_at, 
    p.score,
    (
      SELECT COUNT(*) 
      FROM forum_posts_raw answers 
      WHERE answers.parent_id = p.id 
        AND answers.node_type = 'answer'
        AND (answers.state_string IS NULL OR answers.state_string != '(deleted)')
    ) as answer_count,
    (
      SELECT COUNT(*) 
      FROM forum_posts_raw comments 
      WHERE comments.parent_id = p.id 
        AND comments.node_type = 'comment'
        AND (comments.state_string IS NULL OR comments.state_string != '(deleted)')
    ) as comment_count
  FROM forum_posts_raw p
  ${whereClause}
  GROUP BY p.id, p.title, p.tagnames, p.body, p.node_type, p.added_at, p.score
  ${orderByClause}
  LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`,
  [...params, limit, offset]
);
Key improvements:

Case-insensitive search using LOWER()
Multi-word search support (all terms must match)
Search in related answers/comments
Relevance-based sorting when searching:
Title matches ranked highest
Tag matches ranked second
Body/comment matches ranked third
Partial word matching with LIKE
Maintains original sorting when not searching

"/home/ivanilson_ferreira_u/ayn-rand-forum-viewer/server/src/index.ts""import express from "express";
import cors from "cors";
import dotenv from "dotenv";
import { pool } from "./db";
import { 
  ForumPost, 
  ApiResponse, 
  ForumPostRow, 
  CommentRow, 
  TotalCountRow,
  NodeType,
  SortByValue,
  QueryParams 
} from "./types";

dotenv.config();

const app = express();
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());

const port = process.env.SERVER_PORT || 5000;

// Helper function with proper typing
const buildQueryClauses = (
  search: string,
  nodeType: NodeType,
  sortBy: SortByValue
): { whereClause: string; orderByClause: string; params: any[] } => {
  const params: any[] = [];
  let whereClause = 'WHERE (p.state_string IS NULL OR p.state_string != "(deleted)")';
  
  if (nodeType && nodeType !== 'all') {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = ?';
    params.push(nodeType);
  } else {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = "question"';
  }

  if (search) {
    whereClause += ` AND (
      p.title LIKE ? OR 
      p.body LIKE ? OR 
      p.tagnames LIKE ?
    )`;
    const searchTerm = `%${search}%`;
    params.push(searchTerm, searchTerm, searchTerm);
  }

  let orderByClause = '';
  switch (sortBy) {
    case 'date_asc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY p.added_at ASC';
      break;
    case 'interactions_desc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY (answer_count + comment_count) DESC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'interactions_asc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY (answer_count + comment_count) ASC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'score_desc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY p.score DESC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'score_asc':
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY p.score ASC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    default:
      orderByClause = 'ORDER BY p.added_at DESC';
  }

  return { whereClause, orderByClause, params };
};

app.get("/api/posts", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const page = parseInt(String(req.query.page)) || 1;
    const limit = parseInt(String(req.query.limit)) || 10;
    const search = String(req.query.search || '');
    const nodeType = (req.query.nodeType || 'all') as NodeType;
    const sortBy = (req.query.sortBy || 'date_desc') as SortByValue;
    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;

    const { whereClause, orderByClause, params } = buildQueryClauses(
      search,
      nodeType,
      sortBy
    );

    const [rows] = await pool.query<ForumPostRow[]>(
      `SELECT 
        p.id, 
        p.title, 
        p.tagnames, 
        p.body,
        p.node_type,
        p.added_at, 
        p.score,
        (
          SELECT COUNT(*) 
          FROM forum_posts_raw answers 
          WHERE answers.parent_id = p.id 
            AND answers.node_type = 'answer'
            AND (answers.state_string IS NULL OR answers.state_string != '(deleted)')
        ) as answer_count,
        (
          SELECT COUNT(*) 
          FROM forum_posts_raw comments 
          WHERE comments.parent_id = p.id 
            AND comments.node_type = 'comment'
            AND (comments.state_string IS NULL OR comments.state_string != '(deleted)')
        ) as comment_count
      FROM forum_posts_raw p
      ${whereClause}
      GROUP BY p.id, p.title, p.tagnames, p.body, p.node_type, p.added_at, p.score
      ${orderByClause}
      LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`,
      [...params, limit, offset]
    );

    const [countResult] = await pool.query<TotalCountRow[]>(
      `SELECT COUNT(*) as total 
       FROM forum_posts_raw p
       ${whereClause}`,
      params
    );

    const total = countResult[0].total;
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / limit);

    const formattedRows = rows.map(row => ({
      ...row,
      answer_count: Number(row.answer_count),
      comment_count: Number(row.comment_count)
    }));

    const response: ApiResponse<ForumPost[]> = {
      data: formattedRows,
      total,
      page,
      totalPages,
      filters: {
        search,
        nodeType: nodeType || 'all',
        tags: []
      },
      sort: sortBy
    };

    res.json(response);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Detailed API Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ 
      error: "Internal server error", 
      details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
    });
  }
});

app.get("/api/posts/:postId/comments", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const postId = req.params.postId;
    
    const [post] = await pool.query<ForumPostRow[]>(
      `SELECT id, title, tagnames, body, node_type, added_at, score 
       FROM forum_posts_raw 
       WHERE id = ? AND node_type = 'question'`,
      [postId]
    );

    if (!post[0]) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Post not found" });
    }

    const [comments] = await pool.query<CommentRow[]>(
      `SELECT 
        id,
        body,
        node_type,
        added_at,
        score,
        parent_id
      FROM forum_posts_raw
      WHERE parent_id = ?
        AND node_type IN ('comment', 'answer')
        AND (state_string IS NULL OR state_string != '(deleted)')
      ORDER BY 
        CASE node_type
          WHEN 'answer' THEN 1
          WHEN 'comment' THEN 2
          ELSE 3
        END,
        score DESC,
        added_at ASC`,
      [postId]
    );

    res.json({ 
      comments,
      post: post[0]
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Error fetching comments:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ 
      error: "Internal server error", 
      details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
    });
  }
});

app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server running on port ${port}`);
  console.log(`Environment: ${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'}`);
});

process.on('SIGTERM', async () => {
  console.log('SIGTERM received. Closing database pool...');
  await pool.end();
  process.exit(0);

typescript
CopyInsert
import express from "express";
import cors from "cors";
import dotenv from "dotenv";
import { pool } from "./db";
import { 
  ForumPost, 
  ApiResponse, 
  ForumPostRow, 
  CommentRow, 
  TotalCountRow,
  NodeType,
  SortByValue,
  QueryParams 
} from "./types";

dotenv.config();

const app = express();
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());

const port = process.env.SERVER_PORT || 5000;

const buildQueryClauses = (
  search: string,
  nodeType: NodeType,
  sortBy: SortByValue
): { whereClause: string; orderByClause: string; params: any[] } => {
  const params: any[] = [];
  let whereClause = 'WHERE (p.state_string IS NULL OR p.state_string != "(deleted)")';
  
  // Node type filter
  if (nodeType && nodeType !== 'all') {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = ?';
    params.push(nodeType);
  } else {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = "question"';
  }

  // Enhanced search functionality
  if (search && search.trim()) {
    const searchTerms = search.trim().split(/\s+/).filter(term => term.length > 0);
    if (searchTerms.length > 0) {
      const searchConditions: string[] = [];
      
      searchTerms.forEach(term => {
        // Add each term as a parameter multiple times for different fields
        const searchTerm = `%${term}%`;
        searchConditions.push(`(
          LOWER(p.title) LIKE LOWER(?) OR
          LOWER(p.body) LIKE LOWER(?) OR
          LOWER(p.tagnames) LIKE LOWER(?) OR
          EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 
            FROM forum_posts_raw child 
            WHERE child.parent_id = p.id 
            AND (
              LOWER(child.body) LIKE LOWER(?) OR
              LOWER(child.title) LIKE LOWER(?)
            )
            AND (child.state_string IS NULL OR child.state_string != '(deleted)')
          )
        )`);
        params.push(searchTerm, searchTerm, searchTerm, searchTerm, searchTerm);
      });

      whereClause += ` AND (${searchConditions.join(' AND ')})`;
    }
  }

  // Dynamic ORDER BY clause with search relevance
  let orderByClause = '';
  if (search && search.trim()) {
    const searchTerm = `%${search.trim()}%`;
    orderByClause = `
      ORDER BY
        CASE 
          WHEN LOWER(p.title) LIKE LOWER(?) THEN 4
          WHEN LOWER(p.tagnames) LIKE LOWER(?) THEN 3
          WHEN LOWER(p.body) LIKE LOWER(?) THEN 2
          ELSE 1
        END DESC,
    `;
    params.push(searchTerm, searchTerm, searchTerm);
  }

  // Append regular sort criteria
  switch (sortBy) {
    case 'date_asc':
      orderByClause += orderByClause ? 'p.added_at ASC' : 'ORDER BY p.added_at ASC';
      break;
    case 'interactions_desc':
      orderByClause += orderByClause ? 
        '(answer_count + comment_count) DESC, p.added_at DESC' : 
        'ORDER BY (answer_count + comment_count) DESC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'interactions_asc':
      orderByClause += orderByClause ? 
        '(answer_count + comment_count) ASC, p.added_at DESC' : 
        'ORDER BY (answer_count + comment_count) ASC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'score_desc':
      orderByClause += orderByClause ? 
        'p.score DESC, p.added_at DESC' : 
        'ORDER BY p.score DESC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    case 'score_asc':
      orderByClause += orderByClause ? 
        'p.score ASC, p.added_at DESC' : 
        'ORDER BY p.score ASC, p.added_at DESC';
      break;
    default:
      orderByClause += orderByClause ? 
        'p.added_at DESC' : 
        'ORDER BY p.added_at DESC';
  }

  return { whereClause, orderByClause, params };
};

app.get("/api/posts", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const page = parseInt(String(req.query.page)) || 1;
    const limit = parseInt(String(req.query.limit)) || 10;
    const search = String(req.query.search || '');
    const nodeType = (req.query.nodeType || 'all') as NodeType;
    const sortBy = (req.query.sortBy || 'date_desc') as SortByValue;
    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;

    const { whereClause, orderByClause, params } = buildQueryClauses(
      search,
      nodeType,
      sortBy
    );

    // Main query with enhanced search and counting
    const [rows] = await pool.query<ForumPostRow[]>(
      `SELECT 
        p.id, 
        p.title, 
        p.tagnames, 
        p.body,
        p.node_type,
        p.added_at, 
        p.score,
        (
          SELECT COUNT(*) 
          FROM forum_posts_raw answers 
          WHERE answers.parent_id = p.id 
            AND answers.node_type = 'answer'
            AND (answers.state_string IS NULL OR answers.state_string != '(deleted)')
        ) as answer_count,
        (
          SELECT COUNT(*) 
          FROM forum_posts_raw comments 
          WHERE comments.parent_id = p.id 
            AND comments.node_type = 'comment'
            AND (comments.state_string IS NULL OR comments.state_string != '(deleted)')
        ) as comment_count
      FROM forum_posts_raw p
      ${whereClause}
      GROUP BY p.id, p.title, p.tagnames, p.body, p.node_type, p.added_at, p.score
      ${orderByClause}
      LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`,
      [...params, limit, offset]
    );

    // Count total matching rows
    const [countResult] = await pool.query<TotalCountRow[]>(
      `SELECT COUNT(*) as total 
       FROM forum_posts_raw p
       ${whereClause}`,
      params
    );

    const total = countResult[0].total;
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / limit);

    // Format response
    const formattedRows = rows.map(row => ({
      ...row,
      answer_count: Number(row.answer_count),
      comment_count: Number(row.comment_count)
    }));

    const response: ApiResponse<ForumPost[]> = {
      data: formattedRows,
      total,
      page,
      totalPages,
      filters: {
        search,
        nodeType: nodeType || 'all',
        tags: []
      },
      sort: sortBy
    };

    res.json(response);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Detailed API Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ 
      error: "Internal server error", 
      details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
    });
  }
});

app.get("/api/posts/:postId/comments", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const postId = req.params.postId;
    
    const [post] = await pool.query<ForumPostRow[]>(
      `SELECT id, title, tagnames, body, node_type, added_at, score 
       FROM forum_posts_raw 
       WHERE id = ? AND node_type = 'question'`,
      [postId]
    );

    if (!post[0]) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Post not found" });
    }

    const [comments] = await pool.query<CommentRow[]>(
      `SELECT 
        id,
        body,
        node_type,
        added_at,
        score,
        parent_id
      FROM forum_posts_raw
      WHERE parent_id = ?
        AND node_type IN ('comment', 'answer')
        AND (state_string IS NULL OR state_string != '(deleted)')
      ORDER BY 
        CASE node_type
          WHEN 'answer' THEN 1
          WHEN 'comment' THEN 2
          ELSE 3
        END,
        score DESC,
        added_at ASC`,
      [postId]
    );

    res.json({ 
      comments,
      post: post[0]
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Error fetching comments:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ 
      error: "Internal server error", 
      details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
    });
  }
});

app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server running on port ${port}`);
  console.log(`Environment: ${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'}`);
});

process.on('SIGTERM', async () => {
  console.log('SIGTERM received. Closing database pool...');
  await pool.end();
  process.exit(0);
});

const buildQueryClauses = (
  search: string,
  nodeType: NodeType,
  sortBy: SortByValue
): { whereClause: string; orderByClause: string; params: any[] } => {
  const params: any[] = [];
  let whereClause = 'WHERE (p.state_string IS NULL OR p.state_string != "(deleted)")';
  
  // Modified node type handling
  if (nodeType && nodeType !== 'all') {
    if (nodeType === 'question') {
      whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = "question"';
    } else if (nodeType === 'answer' || nodeType === 'comment') {
      whereClause += ` AND p.node_type = ?`;
      params.push(nodeType);
    }
  } else {
    whereClause += ' AND p.node_type = "question"';
  }

  // Rest of the function remains the same...
};

app.get("/api/posts", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    // ... existing parameters ...

    let query = '';
    if (nodeType === 'answer' || nodeType === 'comment') {
      // Query for answers and comments with their parent post context
      query = `
        SELECT 
          p.id, 
          SUBSTRING(p.body, 1, 150) as title,
          p.tagnames,
          p.body,
          p.node_type,
          p.added_at,
          p.score,
          p.parent_id,
          parent.title as parent_title,
          (
            SELECT COUNT(*) 
            FROM forum_posts_raw answers 
            WHERE answers.parent_id = p.id 
              AND answers.node_type = 'answer'
              AND (answers.state_string IS NULL OR answers.state_string != '(deleted)')
          ) as answer_count,
          (
            SELECT COUNT(*) 
            FROM forum_posts_raw comments 
            WHERE comments.parent_id = p.id 
              AND comments.node_type = 'comment'
              AND (comments.state_string IS NULL OR comments.state_string != '(deleted)')
          ) as comment_count
        FROM forum_posts_raw p
        LEFT JOIN forum_posts_raw parent ON p.parent_id = parent.id
        ${whereClause}
        GROUP BY p.id, p.body, p.tagnames, p.node_type, p.added_at, p.score, p.parent_id, parent.title
        ${orderByClause}
        LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`;
    } else {
      // Existing query for questions
      query = `SELECT 
        p.id, 
        p.title, 
        p.tagnames, 
        p.body,
        p.node_type,
        p.added_at, 
        p.score,
        (
          SELECT COUNT(*) 
          FROM forum_posts_raw answers 
          WHERE answers.parent_id = p.id 
            AND answers.node_type = 'answer'
            AND (answers.state_string IS NULL OR answers.state_string != '(deleted)')
        ) as answer_count,
        (
          SELECT COUNT(*) 
          FROM forum_posts_raw comments 
          WHERE comments.parent_id = p.id 
            AND comments.node_type = 'comment'
            AND (comments.state_string IS NULL OR comments.state_string != '(deleted)')
        ) as comment_count
      FROM forum_posts_raw p
      ${whereClause}
      GROUP BY p.id, p.title, p.tagnames, p.body, p.node_type, p.added_at, p.score
      ${orderByClause}
      LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`;
    }

    const [rows] = await pool.query<ForumPostRow[]>(query, [...params, limit, offset]);

    // Format the titles for answers and comments
    const formattedRows = rows.map(row => ({
      ...row,
      title: row.node_type === 'question' 
        ? row.title 
        : `${row.node_type.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + row.node_type.slice(1)} to: ${row.parent_title || 'Unknown Post'}`,
      answer_count: Number(row.answer_count),
      comment_count: Number(row.comment_count)
    }));

    // Rest of the response handling remains the same...
  }

I apologize for the confusion. Let me explain what we need to do to improve the performance:

First, I've optimized the queries by:
Replacing subqueries with JOINs
Using COALESCE for better NULL handling
Pre-calculating counts in derived tables
We should also add some database indexes to speed up the queries. You'll need to run these SQL commands in your database:

-- Add indexes for faster searches
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_node_type ON forum_posts_raw(node_type);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_parent_id ON forum_posts_raw(parent_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_added_at ON forum_posts_raw(added_at);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_score ON forum_posts_raw(score);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_title_body ON forum_posts_raw(title, body(100));

Take the query structure from last night but enhance it:
sql
CopyInsert
SELECT 
  p.id, 
  p.title, 
  p.tagnames, 
  p.body,
  p.node_type,
  p.added_at, 
  p.score,
  p.parent_id,
  CASE 
    WHEN p.node_type != 'question' THEN 
      (SELECT title FROM forum_posts_raw parent WHERE parent.id = p.parent_id)
    ELSE NULL 
  END as parent_title,
  -- Efficient subqueries for counts
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM forum_posts_raw WHERE parent_id = p.id AND node_type = 'answer' 
   AND (state_string IS NULL OR state_string != '(deleted)')) as answer_count,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM forum_posts_raw WHERE parent_id = p.id AND node_type = 'comment'
   AND (state_string IS NULL OR state_string != '(deleted)')) as comment_count
FROM forum_posts_raw p
${whereClause}
GROUP BY p.id
${orderByClause}
Simplify the title formatting:
typescript
CopyInsert
const formattedRows = rows.map(row => {
  let title = row.title || 'Untitled';
  
  if (row.node_type !== 'question' && row.parent_title) {
    const preview = row.body?.substring(0, 60) || 'No content';
    title = `${row.node_type === 'answer' ? 'Answer' : 'Comment'} to: ${row.parent_title} - ${preview}...`;
  }

  return {
    ...row,
    title,
    answer_count: Number(row.answer_count || 0),
    comment_count: Number(row.comment_count || 0)
  };
});
